\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00093}00093\ \#\ directories\ at\ level\ 8\ which\ is\ the\ default\ and\ also\ the\ maximum\ value.\ The}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00330}00330\ \#\ Doxygen\ selects\ the\ parser\ to\ use\ depending\ on\ the\ extension\ of\ the\ files\ it}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00331}00331\ \#\ parses.\ With\ this\ tag\ you\ can\ assign\ which\ parser\ to\ use\ for\ a\ given}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00332}00332\ \#\ extension.\ Doxygen\ has\ a\ built-\/in\ mapping,\ but\ you\ can\ override\ or\ extend\ it}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00333}00333\ \#\ using\ this\ tag.\ The\ format\ is\ ext=language,\ where\ ext\ is\ a\ file\ extension,\ and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00334}00334\ \#\ language\ is\ one\ of\ the\ parsers\ supported\ by\ doxygen:\ IDL,\ Java,\ JavaScript,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00335}00335\ \#\ Csharp\ (C\#),\ C,\ C++,\ Lex,\ D,\ PHP,\ md\ (Markdown),\ Objective-\/C,\ Python,\ Slice,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00336}00336\ \#\ VHDL,\ Fortran\ (fixed\ format\ Fortran:\ FortranFixed,\ free\ formatted\ Fortran:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00337}00337\ \#\ FortranFree,\ unknown\ formatted\ Fortran:\ Fortran.\ In\ the\ later\ case\ the\ parser}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00338}00338\ \#\ tries\ to\ guess\ whether\ the\ code\ is\ fixed\ or\ free\ formatted\ code,\ this\ is\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00339}00339\ \#\ default\ for\ Fortran\ type\ files).\ For\ instance\ to\ make\ doxygen\ treat\ .inc\ files}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00340}00340\ \#\ as\ Fortran\ files\ (default\ is\ PHP),\ and\ .f\ files\ as\ C\ (default\ is\ Fortran),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00341}00341\ \#\ use:\ inc=Fortran\ f=C.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00342}00342\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00343}00343\ \#\ Note:\ For\ files\ without\ extension\ you\ can\ use\ no\_extension\ as\ a\ placeholder.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00344}00344\ \#}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00481}00481\ \#\ The\ size\ of\ the\ symbol\ lookup\ cache\ can\ be\ set\ using\ LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE.\ This}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00482}00482\ \#\ cache\ is\ used\ to\ resolve\ symbols\ given\ their\ name\ and\ scope.\ Since\ this\ can\ be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00483}00483\ \#\ an\ expensive\ process\ and\ often\ the\ same\ symbol\ appears\ multiple\ times\ in\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00484}00484\ \#\ code,\ doxygen\ keeps\ a\ cache\ of\ pre-\/resolved\ symbols.\ If\ the\ cache\ is\ too\ small}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00485}00485\ \#\ doxygen\ will\ become\ slower.\ If\ the\ cache\ is\ too\ large,\ memory\ is\ wasted.\ The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00486}00486\ \#\ cache\ size\ is\ given\ by\ this\ formula:\ 2\string^(16+LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE).\ The\ valid\ range}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00487}00487\ \#\ is\ 0..9,\ the\ default\ is\ 0,\ corresponding\ to\ a\ cache\ size\ of\ 2\string^16=65536}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00488}00488\ \#\ symbols.\ At\ the\ end\ of\ a\ run\ doxygen\ will\ report\ the\ cache\ usage\ and\ suggest}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00489}00489\ \#\ the\ optimal\ cache\ size\ from\ a\ speed\ point\ of\ view.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00490}00490\ \#\ Minimum\ value:\ 0,\ maximum\ value:\ 9,\ default\ value:\ 0.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00491}00491\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00492}00492\ LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE\ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00493}00493\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00494}00494\ \#\ The\ NUM\_PROC\_THREADS\ specifies\ the\ number\ of\ threads\ doxygen\ is\ allowed\ to\ use}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00495}00495\ \#\ during\ processing.\ When\ set\ to\ 0\ doxygen\ will\ based\ this\ on\ the\ number\ of}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00499}00499\ \#\ threads.\ Since\ this\ is\ still\ an\ experimental\ feature\ the\ default\ is\ set\ to\ 1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00500}00500\ \#\ which\ effectively\ disables\ parallel\ processing.\ Please\ report\ any\ issues\ you}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00896}00896\ \#\ If\ the\ WARN\_AS\_ERROR\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ YES\ then\ doxygen\ will\ immediately\ stop\ when}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00897}00897\ \#\ a\ warning\ is\ encountered.\ If\ the\ WARN\_AS\_ERROR\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00898}00898\ \#\ then\ doxygen\ will\ continue\ running\ as\ if\ WARN\_AS\_ERROR\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ NO,\ but}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00900}00900\ \#\ If\ the\ WARN\_AS\_ERROR\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS\_PRINT\ then\ doxygen\ behaves}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00901}00901\ \#\ like\ FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS\ but\ in\ case\ no\ WARN\_LOGFILE\ is\ defined\ doxygen\ will\ not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00902}00902\ \#\ write\ the\ warning\ messages\ in\ between\ other\ messages\ but\ write\ them\ at\ the\ end}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00903}00903\ \#\ of\ a\ run,\ in\ case\ a\ WARN\_LOGFILE\ is\ defined\ the\ warning\ messages\ will\ be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00904}00904\ \#\ besides\ being\ in\ the\ defined\ file\ also\ be\ shown\ at\ the\ end\ of\ a\ run,\ unless}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00905}00905\ \#\ the\ WARN\_LOGFILE\ is\ defined\ as\ -\/\ i.e.\ standard\ output\ (stdout)\ in\ that\ case}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00906}00906\ \#\ the\ behavior\ will\ remain\ as\ with\ the\ setting\ FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00907}00907\ \#\ Possible\ values\ are:\ NO,\ YES,\ FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS\ and\ FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS\_PRINT.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00908}00908\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00909}00909\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00912}00912\ \#\ The\ WARN\_FORMAT\ tag\ determines\ the\ format\ of\ the\ warning\ messages\ that\ doxygen}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00913}00913\ \#\ can\ produce.\ The\ string\ should\ contain\ the\ \$file,\ \$line,\ and\ \$text\ tags,\ which}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00914}00914\ \#\ will\ be\ replaced\ by\ the\ file\ and\ line\ number\ from\ which\ the\ warning\ originated}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00915}00915\ \#\ and\ the\ warning\ text.\ Optionally\ the\ format\ may\ contain\ \$version,\ which\ will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00916}00916\ \#\ be\ replaced\ by\ the\ version\ of\ the\ file\ (if\ it\ could\ be\ obtained\ via}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00917}00917\ \#\ FILE\_VERSION\_FILTER)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00918}00918\ \#\ See\ also:\ WARN\_LINE\_FORMAT}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00919}00919\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ \$file:\$line:\ \$text.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l00924}00924\ \#\ to\ a\ more\ specific\ place\ is\ given.\ To\ make\ it\ easier\ to\ jump\ to\ this\ place}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01072}01072\ \#\ from\ the\ input.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01079}01079\ \#\ certain\ files\ from\ those\ directories.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01120}01120\ \#\ The\ INPUT\_FILTER\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ specify\ a\ program\ that\ doxygen\ should}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01121}01121\ \#\ invoke\ to\ filter\ for\ each\ input\ file.\ Doxygen\ will\ invoke\ the\ filter\ program}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01122}01122\ \#\ by\ executing\ (via\ popen())\ the\ command:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01123}01123\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01124}01124\ \#\ <filter>\ <input-\/file>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01125}01125\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01126}01126\ \#\ where\ <filter>\ is\ the\ value\ of\ the\ INPUT\_FILTER\ tag,\ and\ <input-\/file>\ is\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01127}01127\ \#\ name\ of\ an\ input\ file.\ Doxygen\ will\ then\ use\ the\ output\ that\ the\ filter}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01128}01128\ \#\ program\ writes\ to\ standard\ output.\ If\ FILTER\_PATTERNS\ is\ specified,\ this\ tag}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01129}01129\ \#\ will\ be\ ignored.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01130}01130\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01131}01131\ \#\ Note\ that\ the\ filter\ must\ not\ add\ or\ remove\ lines;\ it\ is\ applied\ before\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01132}01132\ \#\ code\ is\ scanned,\ but\ not\ when\ the\ output\ code\ is\ generated.\ If\ lines\ are\ added}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01133}01133\ \#\ or\ removed,\ the\ anchors\ will\ not\ be\ placed\ correctly.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01134}01134\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01135}01135\ \#\ Note\ that\ doxygen\ will\ use\ the\ data\ processed\ and\ written\ to\ standard\ output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01136}01136\ \#\ for\ further\ processing,\ therefore\ nothing\ else,\ like\ debug\ statements\ or\ used}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01137}01137\ \#\ commands\ (so\ in\ case\ of\ a\ Windows\ batch\ file\ always\ use\ @echo\ OFF),\ should\ be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01138}01138\ \#\ written\ to\ standard\ output.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01139}01139\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01140}01140\ \#\ Note\ that\ for\ custom\ extensions\ or\ not\ directly\ supported\ extensions\ you\ also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01141}01141\ \#\ need\ to\ set\ EXTENSION\_MAPPING\ for\ the\ extension\ otherwise\ the\ files\ are\ not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01142}01142\ \#\ properly\ processed\ by\ doxygen.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01143}01143\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01144}01144\ INPUT\_FILTER\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01145}01145\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01146}01146\ \#\ The\ FILTER\_PATTERNS\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ specify\ filters\ on\ a\ per\ file\ pattern}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01147}01147\ \#\ basis.\ Doxygen\ will\ compare\ the\ file\ name\ with\ each\ pattern\ and\ apply\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01148}01148\ \#\ filter\ if\ there\ is\ a\ match.\ The\ filters\ are\ a\ list\ of\ the\ form:\ pattern=filter}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01149}01149\ \#\ (like\ *.cpp=my\_cpp\_filter).\ See\ INPUT\_FILTER\ for\ further\ information\ on\ how}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01150}01150\ \#\ filters\ are\ used.\ If\ the\ FILTER\_PATTERNS\ tag\ is\ empty\ or\ if\ none\ of\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01151}01151\ \#\ patterns\ match\ the\ file\ name,\ INPUT\_FILTER\ is\ applied.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01152}01152\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01153}01153\ \#\ Note\ that\ for\ custom\ extensions\ or\ not\ directly\ supported\ extensions\ you\ also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01154}01154\ \#\ need\ to\ set\ EXTENSION\_MAPPING\ for\ the\ extension\ otherwise\ the\ files\ are\ not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01155}01155\ \#\ properly\ processed\ by\ doxygen.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01156}01156\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01181}01181\ \#\ The\ Fortran\ standard\ specifies\ that\ for\ fixed\ formatted\ Fortran\ code\ all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01182}01182\ \#\ characters\ from\ position\ 72\ are\ to\ be\ considered\ as\ comment.\ A\ common}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01183}01183\ \#\ extension\ is\ to\ allow\ longer\ lines\ before\ the\ automatic\ comment\ starts.\ The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01184}01184\ \#\ setting\ FORTRAN\_COMMENT\_AFTER\ will\ also\ make\ it\ possible\ that\ longer\ lines\ can}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01185}01185\ \#\ be\ processed\ before\ the\ automatic\ comment\ starts.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01186}01186\ \#\ Minimum\ value:\ 7,\ maximum\ value:\ 10000,\ default\ value:\ 72.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01187}01187\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01188}01188\ FORTRAN\_COMMENT\_AFTER\ \ =\ 72}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01189}01189\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01238}01238\ \#\ source\ code\ will\ show\ a\ tooltip\ with\ additional\ information\ such\ as\ prototype,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01239}01239\ \#\ brief\ description\ and\ links\ to\ the\ definition\ and\ documentation.\ Since\ this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01240}01240\ \#\ will\ make\ the\ HTML\ file\ larger\ and\ loading\ of\ large\ files\ a\ bit\ slower,\ you}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01249}01249\ \#\ source\ browser.\ The\ htags\ tool\ is\ part\ of\ GNU's\ global\ source\ tagging\ system}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01250}01250\ \#\ (see\ https://www.gnu.org/software/global/global.html).\ You\ will\ need\ version}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01251}01251\ \#\ 4.8.6\ or\ higher.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01252}01252\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01253}01253\ \#\ To\ use\ it\ do\ the\ following:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01254}01254\ \#\ -\/\ Install\ the\ latest\ version\ of\ global}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01255}01255\ \#\ -\/\ Enable\ SOURCE\_BROWSER\ and\ USE\_HTAGS\ in\ the\ configuration\ file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01256}01256\ \#\ -\/\ Make\ sure\ the\ INPUT\ points\ to\ the\ root\ of\ the\ source\ tree}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01257}01257\ \#\ -\/\ Run\ doxygen\ as\ normal}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01258}01258\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01259}01259\ \#\ Doxygen\ will\ invoke\ htags\ (and\ that\ will\ in\ turn\ invoke\ gtags),\ so\ these}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01260}01260\ \#\ tools\ must\ be\ available\ from\ the\ command\ line\ (i.e.\ in\ the\ search\ path).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01261}01261\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01262}01262\ \#\ The\ result:\ instead\ of\ the\ source\ browser\ generated\ by\ doxygen,\ the\ links\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01263}01263\ \#\ source\ code\ will\ now\ point\ to\ the\ output\ of\ htags.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01264}01264\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01265}01265\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ SOURCE\_BROWSER\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01266}01266\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01267}01267\ USE\_HTAGS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01268}01268\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01269}01269\ \#\ If\ the\ VERBATIM\_HEADERS\ tag\ is\ set\ the\ YES\ then\ doxygen\ will\ generate\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01270}01270\ \#\ verbatim\ copy\ of\ the\ header\ file\ for\ each\ class\ for\ which\ an\ include\ is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01271}01271\ \#\ specified.\ Set\ to\ NO\ to\ disable\ this.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01272}01272\ \#\ See\ also:\ Section\ \(\backslash\)class.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01273}01273\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01274}01274\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01275}01275\ VERBATIM\_HEADERS\ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01276}01276\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01277}01277\ \#\ If\ the\ CLANG\_ASSISTED\_PARSING\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ YES\ then\ doxygen\ will\ use\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01278}01278\ \#\ clang\ parser\ (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01279}01279\ \#\ http://clang.llvm.org/)\ for\ more\ accurate\ parsing\ at\ the\ cost\ of\ reduced}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01280}01280\ \#\ performance.\ This\ can\ be\ particularly\ helpful\ with\ template\ rich\ C++\ code\ for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01281}01281\ \#\ which\ doxygen's\ built-\/in\ parser\ lacks\ the\ necessary\ type\ information.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01282}01282\ \#\ Note:\ The\ availability\ of\ this\ option\ depends\ on\ whether\ or\ not\ doxygen\ was}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01283}01283\ \#\ generated\ with\ the\ -\/Duse\_libclang=ON\ option\ for\ CMake.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01284}01284\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01285}01285\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01286}01286\ CLANG\_ASSISTED\_PARSING\ =\ NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01287}01287\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01288}01288\ \#\ If\ the\ CLANG\_ASSISTED\_PARSING\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ YES\ and\ the\ CLANG\_ADD\_INC\_PATHS}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01289}01289\ \#\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ YES\ then\ doxygen\ will\ add\ the\ directory\ of\ each\ input\ to\ the}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01291}01291\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ YES.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01303}01303\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01304}01304\ \#\ If\ clang\ assisted\ parsing\ is\ enabled\ you\ can\ provide\ the\ clang\ parser\ with\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01305}01305\ \#\ path\ to\ the\ directory\ containing\ a\ file\ called\ compile\_commands.json.\ This}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01306}01306\ \#\ file\ is\ the\ compilation\ database\ (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01307}01307\ \#\ http://clang.llvm.org/docs/HowToSetupToolingForLLVM.html)\ containing\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01308}01308\ \#\ options\ used\ when\ the\ source\ files\ were\ built.\ This\ is\ equivalent\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01309}01309\ \#\ specifying\ the\ -\/p\ option\ to\ a\ clang\ tool,\ such\ as\ clang-\/check.\ These\ options}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01311}01311\ \#\ will\ be\ added\ as\ well.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01312}01312\ \#\ Note:\ The\ availability\ of\ this\ option\ depends\ on\ whether\ or\ not\ doxygen\ was}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01372}01372\ \#\ for\ information\ on\ how\ to\ generate\ the\ default\ header\ that\ doxygen\ normally}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01392}01392\ \#\ sheet\ that\ is\ used\ by\ each\ HTML\ page.\ It\ can\ be\ used\ to\ fine-\/tune\ the\ look\ of}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01395}01395\ \#\ sheet\ that\ doxygen\ normally\ uses.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01396}01396\ \#\ Note:\ It\ is\ recommended\ to\ use\ HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET\ instead\ of\ this\ tag,\ as}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01397}01397\ \#\ it\ is\ more\ robust\ and\ this\ tag\ (HTML\_STYLESHEET)\ will\ in\ the\ future\ become}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01398}01398\ \#\ obsolete.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01401}01401\ HTML\_STYLESHEET\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01402}01402\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01403}01403\ \#\ The\ HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ specify\ additional\ user-\/defined}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01404}01404\ \#\ cascading\ style\ sheets\ that\ are\ included\ after\ the\ standard\ style\ sheets}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01405}01405\ \#\ created\ by\ doxygen.\ Using\ this\ option\ one\ can\ overrule\ certain\ style\ aspects.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01406}01406\ \#\ This\ is\ preferred\ over\ using\ HTML\_STYLESHEET\ since\ it\ does\ not\ replace\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01407}01407\ \#\ standard\ style\ sheet\ and\ is\ therefore\ more\ robust\ against\ future\ updates.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01408}01408\ \#\ Doxygen\ will\ copy\ the\ style\ sheet\ files\ to\ the\ output\ directory.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01409}01409\ \#\ Note:\ The\ order\ of\ the\ extra\ style\ sheet\ files\ is\ of\ importance\ (e.g.\ the\ last}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01410}01410\ \#\ style\ sheet\ in\ the\ list\ overrules\ the\ setting\ of\ the\ previous\ ones\ in\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01411}01411\ \#\ list).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01412}01412\ \#\ Note:\ Since\ the\ styling\ of\ scrollbars\ can\ currently\ not\ be\ overruled\ in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01413}01413\ \#\ Webkit/Chromium,\ the\ styling\ will\ be\ left\ out\ of\ the\ default\ doxygen.css\ if}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01414}01414\ \#\ one\ or\ more\ extra\ stylesheets\ have\ been\ specified.\ So\ if\ scrollbar}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01415}01415\ \#\ customization\ is\ desired\ it\ has\ to\ be\ added\ explicitly.\ For\ an\ example\ see\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01416}01416\ \#\ documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01417}01417\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_HTML\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01418}01418\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01419}01419\ HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET\ \ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01420}01420\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01431}01431\ \#\ The\ HTML\_COLORSTYLE\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ specify\ if\ the\ generated\ HTML\ output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01432}01432\ \#\ should\ be\ rendered\ with\ a\ dark\ or\ light\ theme.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01433}01433\ \#\ Possible\ values\ are:\ LIGHT\ always\ generate\ light\ mode\ output,\ DARK\ always}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01434}01434\ \#\ generate\ dark\ mode\ output,\ AUTO\_LIGHT\ automatically\ set\ the\ mode\ according\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01435}01435\ \#\ the\ user\ preference,\ use\ light\ mode\ if\ no\ preference\ is\ set\ (the\ default),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01436}01436\ \#\ AUTO\_DARK\ automatically\ set\ the\ mode\ according\ to\ the\ user\ preference,\ use}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01437}01437\ \#\ dark\ mode\ if\ no\ preference\ is\ set\ and\ TOGGLE\ allow\ to\ user\ to\ switch\ between}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01438}01438\ \#\ light\ and\ dark\ mode\ via\ a\ button.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01439}01439\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ AUTO\_LIGHT.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01440}01440\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_HTML\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01444}01444\ \#\ The\ HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_HUE\ tag\ controls\ the\ color\ of\ the\ HTML\ output.\ Doxygen}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01445}01445\ \#\ will\ adjust\ the\ colors\ in\ the\ style\ sheet\ and\ background\ images\ according\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01446}01446\ \#\ this\ color.\ Hue\ is\ specified\ as\ an\ angle\ on\ a\ color-\/wheel,\ see}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01447}01447\ \#\ https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hue\ for\ more\ information.\ For\ instance\ the\ value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01448}01448\ \#\ 0\ represents\ red,\ 60\ is\ yellow,\ 120\ is\ green,\ 180\ is\ cyan,\ 240\ is\ blue,\ 300}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01449}01449\ \#\ purple,\ and\ 360\ is\ red\ again.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01450}01450\ \#\ Minimum\ value:\ 0,\ maximum\ value:\ 359,\ default\ value:\ 220.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01451}01451\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_HTML\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01455}01455\ \#\ The\ HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_SAT\ tag\ controls\ the\ purity\ (or\ saturation)\ of\ the\ colors}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01456}01456\ \#\ in\ the\ HTML\ output.\ For\ a\ value\ of\ 0\ the\ output\ will\ use\ gray-\/scales\ only.\ A}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01457}01457\ \#\ value\ of\ 255\ will\ produce\ the\ most\ vivid\ colors.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01463}01463\ \#\ The\ HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_GAMMA\ tag\ controls\ the\ gamma\ correction\ applied\ to\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01464}01464\ \#\ luminance\ component\ of\ the\ colors\ in\ the\ HTML\ output.\ Values\ below\ 100}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01465}01465\ \#\ gradually\ make\ the\ output\ lighter,\ whereas\ values\ above\ 100\ make\ the\ output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01466}01466\ \#\ darker.\ The\ value\ divided\ by\ 100\ is\ the\ actual\ gamma\ applied,\ so\ 80\ represents}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01467}01467\ \#\ a\ gamma\ of\ 0.8,\ The\ value\ 220\ represents\ a\ gamma\ of\ 2.2,\ and\ 100\ does\ not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01468}01468\ \#\ change\ the\ gamma.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01469}01469\ \#\ Minimum\ value:\ 40,\ maximum\ value:\ 240,\ default\ value:\ 80.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01470}01470\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_HTML\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01471}01471\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01594}01594\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01595}01595\ \#\ The\ HTML\ Help\ Workshop\ contains\ a\ compiler\ that\ can\ convert\ all\ HTML\ output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01596}01596\ \#\ generated\ by\ doxygen\ into\ a\ single\ compiled\ HTML\ file\ (.chm).\ Compiled\ HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01597}01597\ \#\ files\ are\ now\ used\ as\ the\ Windows\ 98\ help\ format,\ and\ will\ replace\ the\ old}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01598}01598\ \#\ Windows\ help\ format\ (.hlp)\ on\ all\ Windows\ platforms\ in\ the\ future.\ Compressed}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01599}01599\ \#\ HTML\ files\ also\ contain\ an\ index,\ a\ table\ of\ contents,\ and\ you\ can\ search\ for}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01744}01744\ \#\ If\ you\ want\ full\ control\ over\ the\ layout\ of\ the\ generated\ HTML\ pages\ it\ might}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01745}01745\ \#\ be\ necessary\ to\ disable\ the\ index\ and\ replace\ it\ with\ your\ own.\ The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01746}01746\ \#\ DISABLE\_INDEX\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ turn\ on/off\ the\ condensed\ index\ (tabs)\ at\ top}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01747}01747\ \#\ of\ each\ HTML\ page.\ A\ value\ of\ NO\ enables\ the\ index\ and\ the\ value\ YES\ disables}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01748}01748\ \#\ it.\ Since\ the\ tabs\ in\ the\ index\ contain\ the\ same\ information\ as\ the\ navigation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01749}01749\ \#\ tree,\ you\ can\ set\ this\ option\ to\ YES\ if\ you\ also\ set\ GENERATE\_TREEVIEW\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01750}01750\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01751}01751\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_HTML\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01754}01754\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01755}01755\ \#\ The\ GENERATE\_TREEVIEW\ tag\ is\ used\ to\ specify\ whether\ a\ tree-\/like\ index}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01756}01756\ \#\ structure\ should\ be\ generated\ to\ display\ hierarchical\ information.\ If\ the\ tag}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01757}01757\ \#\ value\ is\ set\ to\ YES,\ a\ side\ panel\ will\ be\ generated\ containing\ a\ tree-\/like}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01758}01758\ \#\ index\ structure\ (just\ like\ the\ one\ that\ is\ generated\ for\ HTML\ Help).\ For\ this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01759}01759\ \#\ to\ work\ a\ browser\ that\ supports\ JavaScript,\ DHTML,\ CSS\ and\ frames\ is\ required}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01760}01760\ \#\ (i.e.\ any\ modern\ browser).\ Windows\ users\ are\ probably\ better\ off\ using\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01761}01761\ \#\ HTML\ help\ feature.\ Via\ custom\ style\ sheets\ (see\ HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET)\ one\ can}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01762}01762\ \#\ further\ fine\ tune\ the\ look\ of\ the\ index\ (see\ "{}Fine-\/tuning\ the\ output"{}).\ As\ an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01763}01763\ \#\ example,\ the\ default\ style\ sheet\ generated\ by\ doxygen\ has\ an\ example\ that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01764}01764\ \#\ shows\ how\ to\ put\ an\ image\ at\ the\ root\ of\ the\ tree\ instead\ of\ the\ PROJECT\_NAME.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01765}01765\ \#\ Since\ the\ tree\ basically\ has\ the\ same\ information\ as\ the\ tab\ index,\ you\ could}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01766}01766\ \#\ consider\ setting\ DISABLE\_INDEX\ to\ YES\ when\ enabling\ this\ option.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01767}01767\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01768}01768\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_HTML\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01769}01769\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01770}01770\ GENERATE\_TREEVIEW\ \ \ \ \ \ =\ NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01771}01771\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01772}01772\ \#\ When\ both\ GENERATE\_TREEVIEW\ and\ DISABLE\_INDEX\ are\ set\ to\ YES,\ then\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01773}01773\ \#\ FULL\_SIDEBAR\ option\ determines\ if\ the\ side\ bar\ is\ limited\ to\ only\ the\ treeview}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01774}01774\ \#\ area\ (value\ NO)\ or\ if\ it\ should\ extend\ to\ the\ full\ height\ of\ the\ window\ (value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01775}01775\ \#\ YES).\ Setting\ this\ to\ YES\ gives\ a\ layout\ similar\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01776}01776\ \#\ https://docs.readthedocs.io\ with\ more\ room\ for\ contents,\ but\ less\ room\ for\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01777}01777\ \#\ project\ logo,\ title,\ and\ description.\ If\ either\ GENERATE\_TREEVIEW\ or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01778}01778\ \#\ DISABLE\_INDEX\ is\ set\ to\ NO,\ this\ option\ has\ no\ effect.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01915}01915\ \#\ When\ the\ SEARCHENGINE\ tag\ is\ enabled\ doxygen\ will\ generate\ a\ search\ box\ for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01916}01916\ \#\ the\ HTML\ output.\ The\ underlying\ search\ engine\ uses\ javascript\ and\ DHTML\ and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01917}01917\ \#\ should\ work\ on\ any\ modern\ browser.\ Note\ that\ when\ using\ HTML\ help}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01918}01918\ \#\ (GENERATE\_HTMLHELP),\ Qt\ help\ (GENERATE\_QHP),\ or\ docsets\ (GENERATE\_DOCSET)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01919}01919\ \#\ there\ is\ already\ a\ search\ function\ so\ this\ one\ should\ typically\ be\ disabled.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01920}01920\ \#\ For\ large\ projects\ the\ javascript\ based\ search\ engine\ can\ be\ slow,\ then}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01921}01921\ \#\ enabling\ SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH\ may\ provide\ a\ better\ solution.\ It\ is\ possible\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01922}01922\ \#\ search\ using\ the\ keyboard;\ to\ jump\ to\ the\ search\ box\ use\ <access\ key>\ +\ S}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01923}01923\ \#\ (what\ the\ <access\ key>\ is\ depends\ on\ the\ OS\ and\ browser,\ but\ it\ is\ typically}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01924}01924\ \#\ <CTRL>,\ <ALT>/<option>,\ or\ both).\ Inside\ the\ search\ box\ use\ the\ <cursor\ down}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01925}01925\ \#\ key>\ to\ jump\ into\ the\ search\ results\ window,\ the\ results\ can\ be\ navigated}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01926}01926\ \#\ using\ the\ <cursor\ keys>.\ Press\ <Enter>\ to\ select\ an\ item\ or\ <escape>\ to\ cancel}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01927}01927\ \#\ the\ search.\ The\ filter\ options\ can\ be\ selected\ when\ the\ cursor\ is\ inside\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01928}01928\ \#\ search\ box\ by\ pressing\ <Shift>+<cursor\ down>.\ Also\ here\ use\ the\ <cursor\ keys>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01929}01929\ \#\ to\ select\ a\ filter\ and\ <Enter>\ or\ <escape>\ to\ activate\ or\ cancel\ the\ filter}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01930}01930\ \#\ option.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01931}01931\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01932}01932\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_HTML\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01933}01933\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01934}01934\ SEARCHENGINE\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01935}01935\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01936}01936\ \#\ When\ the\ SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH\ tag\ is\ enabled\ the\ search\ engine\ will\ be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01937}01937\ \#\ implemented\ using\ a\ web\ server\ instead\ of\ a\ web\ client\ using\ JavaScript.\ There}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01938}01938\ \#\ are\ two\ flavors\ of\ web\ server\ based\ searching\ depending\ on\ the\ EXTERNAL\_SEARCH}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01939}01939\ \#\ setting.\ When\ disabled,\ doxygen\ will\ generate\ a\ PHP\ script\ for\ searching\ and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01940}01940\ \#\ an\ index\ file\ used\ by\ the\ script.\ When\ EXTERNAL\_SEARCH\ is\ enabled\ the\ indexing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01941}01941\ \#\ and\ searching\ needs\ to\ be\ provided\ by\ external\ tools.\ See\ the\ section}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01942}01942\ \#\ "{}External\ Indexing\ and\ Searching"{}\ for\ details.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01943}01943\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01944}01944\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ SEARCHENGINE\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01945}01945\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01946}01946\ SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH\ \ \ \ =\ NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01947}01947\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01948}01948\ \#\ When\ EXTERNAL\_SEARCH\ tag\ is\ enabled\ doxygen\ will\ no\ longer\ generate\ the\ PHP}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01949}01949\ \#\ script\ for\ searching.\ Instead\ the\ search\ results\ are\ written\ to\ an\ XML\ file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01950}01950\ \#\ which\ needs\ to\ be\ processed\ by\ an\ external\ indexer.\ Doxygen\ will\ invoke\ an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01951}01951\ \#\ external\ search\ engine\ pointed\ to\ by\ the\ SEARCHENGINE\_URL\ option\ to\ obtain\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01952}01952\ \#\ search\ results.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01953}01953\ \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01954}01954\ \#\ Doxygen\ ships\ with\ an\ example\ indexer\ (doxyindexer)\ and\ search\ engine}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01955}01955\ \#\ (doxysearch.cgi)\ which\ are\ based\ on\ the\ open\ source\ search\ engine\ library}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01956}01956\ \#\ Xapian\ (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01957}01957\ \#\ https://xapian.org/).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l01958}01958\ \#}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02129}02129\ \#\ If\ the\ PDF\_HYPERLINKS\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ YES,\ the\ LaTeX\ that\ is\ generated\ is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02130}02130\ \#\ prepared\ for\ conversion\ to\ PDF\ (using\ ps2pdf\ or\ pdflatex).\ The\ PDF\ file\ will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02131}02131\ \#\ contain\ links\ (just\ like\ the\ HTML\ output)\ instead\ of\ page\ references.\ This}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02132}02132\ \#\ makes\ the\ output\ suitable\ for\ online\ browsing\ using\ a\ PDF\ viewer.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02148}02148\ \#\ The\ LATEX\_BATCHMODE\ tag\ signals\ the\ behavior\ of\ LaTeX\ in\ case\ of\ an\ error.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02149}02149\ \#\ Possible\ values\ are:\ NO\ same\ as\ ERROR\_STOP,\ YES\ same\ as\ BATCH,\ BATCH\ In\ batch}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02150}02150\ \#\ mode\ nothing\ is\ printed\ on\ the\ terminal,\ errors\ are\ scrolled\ as\ if\ <return>\ is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02151}02151\ \#\ hit\ at\ every\ error;\ missing\ files\ that\ TeX\ tries\ to\ input\ or\ request\ from}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02152}02152\ \#\ keyboard\ input\ (\(\backslash\)read\ on\ a\ not\ open\ input\ stream)\ cause\ the\ job\ to\ abort,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02153}02153\ \#\ NON\_STOP\ In\ nonstop\ mode\ the\ diagnostic\ message\ will\ appear\ on\ the\ terminal,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02154}02154\ \#\ but\ there\ is\ no\ possibility\ of\ user\ interaction\ just\ like\ in\ batch\ mode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02155}02155\ \#\ SCROLL\ In\ scroll\ mode,\ TeX\ will\ stop\ only\ for\ missing\ files\ to\ input\ or\ if}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02156}02156\ \#\ keyboard\ input\ is\ necessary\ and\ ERROR\_STOP\ In\ errorstop\ mode,\ TeX\ will\ stop\ at}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02157}02157\ \#\ each\ error,\ asking\ for\ user\ intervention.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02158}02158\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02159}02159\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ GENERATE\_LATEX\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02160}02160\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02449}02449\ \#\ contain\ include\ files\ that\ are\ not\ input\ files\ but\ should\ be\ processed\ by\ the}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02456}02456\ \#\ You\ can\ use\ the\ INCLUDE\_FILE\_PATTERNS\ tag\ to\ specify\ one\ or\ more\ wildcard}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02457}02457\ \#\ patterns\ (like\ *.h\ and\ *.hpp)\ to\ filter\ out\ the\ header-\/files\ in\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02458}02458\ \#\ directories.\ If\ left\ blank,\ the\ patterns\ specified\ with\ FILE\_PATTERNS\ will\ be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02459}02459\ \#\ used.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02463}02463\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02464}02464\ \#\ The\ PREDEFINED\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ specify\ one\ or\ more\ macro\ names\ that\ are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02465}02465\ \#\ defined\ before\ the\ preprocessor\ is\ started\ (similar\ to\ the\ -\/D\ option\ of\ e.g.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02466}02466\ \#\ gcc).\ The\ argument\ of\ the\ tag\ is\ a\ list\ of\ macros\ of\ the\ form:\ name\ or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02467}02467\ \#\ name=definition\ (no\ spaces).\ If\ the\ definition\ and\ the\ "{}="{}\ are\ omitted,\ "{}=1"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02468}02468\ \#\ is\ assumed.\ To\ prevent\ a\ macro\ definition\ from\ being\ undefined\ via\ \#undef\ or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02469}02469\ \#\ recursively\ expanded\ use\ the\ :=\ operator\ instead\ of\ the\ =\ operator.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02470}02470\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02471}02471\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02472}02472\ PREDEFINED\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02473}02473\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02474}02474\ \#\ If\ the\ MACRO\_EXPANSION\ and\ EXPAND\_ONLY\_PREDEF\ tags\ are\ set\ to\ YES\ then\ this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02475}02475\ \#\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ specify\ a\ list\ of\ macro\ names\ that\ should\ be\ expanded.\ The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02476}02476\ \#\ macro\ definition\ that\ is\ found\ in\ the\ sources\ will\ be\ used.\ Use\ the\ PREDEFINED}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02477}02477\ \#\ tag\ if\ you\ want\ to\ use\ a\ different\ macro\ definition\ that\ overrules\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02478}02478\ \#\ definition\ found\ in\ the\ source\ code.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02479}02479\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02480}02480\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02481}02481\ EXPAND\_AS\_DEFINED\ \ \ \ \ \ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02482}02482\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02483}02483\ \#\ If\ the\ SKIP\_FUNCTION\_MACROS\ tag\ is\ set\ to\ YES\ then\ doxygen's\ preprocessor\ will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02484}02484\ \#\ remove\ all\ references\ to\ function-\/like\ macros\ that\ are\ alone\ on\ a\ line,\ have}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02485}02485\ \#\ an\ all\ uppercase\ name,\ and\ do\ not\ end\ with\ a\ semicolon.\ Such\ function\ macros}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02486}02486\ \#\ are\ typically\ used\ for\ boiler-\/plate\ code,\ and\ will\ confuse\ the\ parser\ if\ not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02487}02487\ \#\ removed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02488}02488\ \#\ The\ default\ value\ is:\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02489}02489\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02490}02490\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02491}02491\ SKIP\_FUNCTION\_MACROS\ \ \ =\ YES}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02497}02497\ \#\ The\ TAGFILES\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ specify\ one\ or\ more\ tag\ files.\ For\ each\ tag}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02498}02498\ \#\ file\ the\ location\ of\ the\ external\ documentation\ should\ be\ added.\ The\ format\ of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02499}02499\ \#\ a\ tag\ file\ without\ this\ location\ is\ as\ follows:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02500}02500\ \#\ TAGFILES\ =\ file1\ file2\ ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02501}02501\ \#\ Adding\ location\ for\ the\ tag\ files\ is\ done\ as\ follows:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02502}02502\ \#\ TAGFILES\ =\ file1=loc1\ "{}file2\ =\ loc2"{}\ ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02503}02503\ \#\ where\ loc1\ and\ loc2\ can\ be\ relative\ or\ absolute\ paths\ or\ URLs.\ See\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02504}02504\ \#\ section\ "{}Linking\ to\ external\ documentation"{}\ for\ more\ information\ about\ the\ use}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02505}02505\ \#\ of\ tag\ files.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02506}02506\ \#\ Note:\ Each\ tag\ file\ must\ have\ a\ unique\ name\ (where\ the\ name\ does\ NOT\ include}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02507}02507\ \#\ the\ path).\ If\ a\ tag\ file\ is\ not\ located\ in\ the\ directory\ in\ which\ doxygen\ is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02508}02508\ \#\ run,\ you\ must\ also\ specify\ the\ path\ to\ the\ tagfile\ here.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02509}02509\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02511}02511\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02657}02657\ \#\ is\ enforced.\ So\ when\ you\ set\ the\ threshold\ to\ 10,\ up\ to\ 15\ fields\ may\ appear,}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02839}02839\ \#\ The\ DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ set\ the\ maximum\ number\ of\ nodes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02840}02840\ \#\ that\ will\ be\ shown\ in\ the\ graph.\ If\ the\ number\ of\ nodes\ in\ a\ graph\ becomes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02841}02841\ \#\ larger\ than\ this\ value,\ doxygen\ will\ truncate\ the\ graph,\ which\ is\ visualized}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02842}02842\ \#\ by\ representing\ a\ node\ as\ a\ red\ box.\ Note\ that\ doxygen\ if\ the\ number\ of\ direct}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02843}02843\ \#\ children\ of\ the\ root\ node\ in\ a\ graph\ is\ already\ larger\ than}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02844}02844\ \#\ DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES\ then\ the\ graph\ will\ not\ be\ shown\ at\ all.\ Also\ note\ that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02845}02845\ \#\ the\ size\ of\ a\ graph\ can\ be\ further\ restricted\ by\ MAX\_DOT\_GRAPH\_DEPTH.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02846}02846\ \#\ Minimum\ value:\ 0,\ maximum\ value:\ 10000,\ default\ value:\ 50.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02847}02847\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ HAVE\_DOT\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02848}02848\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02851}02851\ \#\ The\ MAX\_DOT\_GRAPH\_DEPTH\ tag\ can\ be\ used\ to\ set\ the\ maximum\ depth\ of\ the\ graphs}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02852}02852\ \#\ generated\ by\ dot.\ A\ depth\ value\ of\ 3\ means\ that\ only\ nodes\ reachable\ from\ the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02853}02853\ \#\ root\ by\ following\ a\ path\ via\ at\ most\ 3\ edges\ will\ be\ shown.\ Nodes\ that\ lay}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02854}02854\ \#\ further\ from\ the\ root\ node\ will\ be\ omitted.\ Note\ that\ setting\ this\ option\ to\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02855}02855\ \#\ or\ 2\ may\ greatly\ reduce\ the\ computation\ time\ needed\ for\ large\ code\ bases.\ Also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02856}02856\ \#\ note\ that\ the\ size\ of\ a\ graph\ can\ be\ further\ restricted\ by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02857}02857\ \#\ DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES.\ Using\ a\ depth\ of\ 0\ means\ no\ depth\ restriction.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02858}02858\ \#\ Minimum\ value:\ 0,\ maximum\ value:\ 1000,\ default\ value:\ 0.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02859}02859\ \#\ This\ tag\ requires\ that\ the\ tag\ HAVE\_DOT\ is\ set\ to\ YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_doxyfile_source_l02860}02860\ }
